Weixian

Qin and Han Bricks and Tiles Sold to Japanese Again 93

Transported to Qingdao and Detained

Provincial Library Urgently Seeks to Rescue Them

Jinan Correspondence: Recently, news of the loss of Shandong antiquities has been constantly reported. The Haiyuan Pavilion Library of the Yang family in Liaocheng was destroyed and sold previously, and the Tibetan scriptures of the Hainan Temple in Yexian were destroyed later, which are truly major misfortunes for Shandong's culture. Unexpectedly, one wave subsides, and another rises. The Haiyuan Pavilion Library was sold to the Japanese and is about to flow into a foreign country. Now, seven or eight hundred Qin and Han bricks and tiles collected by the Gao family in Weixian have been sold to the Japanese. It is extremely distressing. Fortunately, the pottery was transported to Qingdao by the Japanese and detained and inspected by the station there. The Shandong Provincial Library has sent letters to various agencies in Qingdao, stating that these bricks and tiles are the essence of ancient bricks and tiles of all of China and requesting their detention to jointly discuss proper methods of preservation. At the same time, it has requested the Shandong Department of Education to immediately telegraph the Qingdao Municipal Government and the Jiaoji Railway Administration to handle everything. The details of this case are recorded as follows:

History of Bricks and Tiles 94

During the Qing Dynasty, there was a Gao Qingling in Weixian who was a preserver of antiquities. He collected about seven or eight hundred Qin and Han bricks and tiles, all of which were unique masterpieces and the essence of ancient bricks and tiles in the country. Gao believed that these bricks and tiles were valuable and precious, and he wrote a special book, "Wen Xun of Shangtao Studio Bricks and Tiles," which recorded the matter in detail, totaling twenty-four large volumes, all of which were rubbings. About two feet long and eight inches wide, the Shandong Library purchased a copy for 250 yuan, and the value of the bricks and tiles is truly no different from the Jade of Liancheng.

Sold to Japanese 95

Recently, two or three days ago, the descendants of Gao Qingling were unable to inherit their ancestors' legacy and sold all of these Qin and Han bricks and tiles to the Japanese. Yesterday, the Japanese packed these bricks and tiles into more than fifty large boxes and transported them out of Weixian. When they arrived in Qingdao, the Qingdao Station of the Jiaoji Railway detained them for inspection, but few people recognize the value of these bricks and tiles, so it is still unknown whether they will be shipped out now.

Urgently Seeking Rescue 96

The Shandong Provincial Library, upon receiving this news, believed that the matter concerned the pottery culture and history of China and could not allow it to fall into foreign hands. Therefore, the library sent separate urgent letters to the Qingdao Municipal Government, the Jiaoji Railway Management Committee, the Bureau of Education, and the Bureau of Social Affairs, stating that these bricks and tiles were of great importance and requested that they be detained and preserved according to the Law on the Preservation of Antiquities. At the same time, it reported to the Department of Education and requested that it telegraph the Qingdao Municipal Government and the Jiaoji Railway Management Committee to detain these bricks and tiles. The Shandong Library wrote to the Qingdao Municipal Government, etc., stating, "To whom it may concern, the large number of bricks and tiles collected by the Gao family in Weixian are the only national treasures among the pottery in the country. There is a special book named 'Wen Xun of Shangtao Studio Bricks and Tiles,' which is well-known in academic circles. We have recently heard that a national of a certain country has bought them and is about to export them to Qingdao. This matter concerns the pottery culture of the entire nation, and we dare not remain silent. Please investigate and seize them in accordance with the Law on the Preservation of Antiquities promulgated by the National Government and preserve them for the public. We would be most grateful." (20th)

News of Reorganization of Hubei Provincial Government 97

Wuhan Municipal Government to Merge with Provincial Government

Hankou Correspondence: The Hubei Provincial Government, since its establishment last year, has been unable to support its military and political expenses due to the abolition of likin and the sharp decline in tax revenue. On the other hand, Hankou's income has exceeded the provincial tax revenue, and the idea of merging the province and the city has become quite popular. Recently, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, He Chengjun, and the Mayor of Hankou, Liu Wendao, went to Beijing one after another to report the administrative situation to Chairman Jiang. As a result, the issue of a partial reorganization of the provincial government and the abolition of the municipal government has arisen due to the merging of the province and city. The Provincial Government Committee consists of nine members: Chairman He Chengjun, who concurrently serves as Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Wu Xingya, who concurrently serves as Director of the Department of Finance, Zhang Guanshi, who concurrently serves as Director of the Department of Construction, Fang Dazhi, who concurrently serves as Director of the Department of Education, Huang Jianzhong, who concurrently serves as Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, Peng Jieshi, Committee members Chen Guangzu, Xiong Bingkun, and Xie Lü, etc. On the municipal government side, the Secretary-General is He Fuzhou, the Director of the Bureau of Social Affairs is Yang Zaichun, the Director of the Bureau of Public Utilities is Huang Zhenxing, the Director of the Bureau of Finance is Wu Guozhen, the Director of the Bureau of Education is Liu Wendao, and the Director of the Bureau of Public Works is Chen Keming, etc. After the merging of the province and city, the issue of who will stay and who will go has become a major concern. It is rumored that the new provincial government will still be headed by He Chengjun as chairman, Liu Wendao as Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and Wu Guozhen as Director of the Department of Finance. The Departments of Construction and Education will remain unchanged. The Hankou Municipal Government will be reorganized into an ordinary city directly under the provincial government, and the position of mayor will be selected from Chen Guangzu, Chen Keming, and Huang Zhenxing. Wu Xingya, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, will be transferred back to his original position as Director of the Department of Civil Affairs in Anhui, and Zhang Guanshi, Director of the Department of Finance, will be allowed to resign. However, when questioned by the parties involved, they all denied it. It is likely that the central government will have to make a decision before it can be revealed. It is heard that the entire Provincial Government Committee has jointly telegraphed the central government on the 20th, submitting their resignations, and those who concurrently hold positions as department or bureau directors have also telegraphed Beijing to resign individually. Strike Wave at British-Owned Tobacco Company in Hankou

Municipal Government Negotiations Ineffective

Workers to Stage General Strike

Hankou Correspondence: Workers in the printing department of the British-owned British American Tobacco Company in Hankou were not paid wages and had their rice subsidies deducted by the factory for attending the National Assembly elections and taking leave for the May 5th Memorial Day holiday. The workers requested the factory authorities to pay wages according to the methods of other factories for more than twenty days, but the factory did not allow it. The Tobacco Guild presented the matter to the party, government, and military authorities, requesting them to mediate, but it was unsuccessful. Unexpectedly, the factory authorities suddenly closed the main switch of the electric motor, refusing workers to enter the factory, and announced a shutdown at 5:00 PM on the 19th. The announcement stated, "British American Tobacco Company Printing Department Announcement: The head office has refused to pay wages for April 15th and May 5th. The factory will be shut down from today. This announcement is for your information." Liu then invited the Five-Province Diplomatic Inspector Zhou Zechun to discuss solutions for further negotiations with the British Consul. As for the workers, they are strictly observing discipline, and workers from other departments will also automatically strike to provide assistance. If the British side does not make concessions, the disturbance may be difficult to contain. (May 21st)

A True Record of the Important Border Affairs of Yunnan and Burma 98

The Lower Section of the Kokang Tusi Being Occupied by the British

After Burma was conquered by the British, it is unknown how many tens of millions of miles of Yunnan's border areas were lost as a result. Of these tens of millions of miles, from Simao, Kaijiang, and Xiaohe in the upper section to Gunlu, Jiangnan, and Banjiangkou in the lower section, it can be divided into three sections. The people of the country are fully aware of the upper section from Langsu to Xidong. In the middle section from Shenhu Pass, Wanren Pass, Jushi Pass, Tongbi Pass, Tiebi Pass, Huju Pass, Tianma Pass, to Nankan Hanlong Pass, the Tengyue Road and the British Consul meet once a year to resolve all disputes among the people. Although foreigners sometimes move the border markers, there is no major harm. However, the lower section from Lujiang Mengbang Zhugeliying to Nanbanjiangkou is extremely important. A certain gentleman who has traveled to the area to investigate has written a diary, and we have selected the main points for the reference of our fellow countrymen.

Area and Population 99

The undetermined border section between Yunnan and Burma is collectively known as the "Five Five District," which includes the territories under the jurisdiction of thirteen Tusi. The thirteen Tusi are Laxmen, Mumeng, Gengma, Dedang, Xiaomengtong, Mengpeng, Mengli, Mengding, Menglang, Kokang, Gongmeng, Gangmeng, and the raw, uncivilized lands. The territories under the jurisdiction of each Tusi vary in size. The larger ones are Gengma and the raw, uncivilized lands, each with a territory of about a thousand li in length and width. The smaller ones are Mumeng, Dedang, Mengli, Menglang, Gongmeng, and Gangmeng, each with a territory of about four hundred li in length and width. In total, the territories under the jurisdiction of the thirteen Tusi are about ten thousand li in length and width. In other words, the undetermined border section between Yunnan and Burma is about ten thousand li in length and width. Since this section is located in a remote area, the population is naturally sparse. Large Tusi like Gengma can have more than ten thousand households, while small Tusi like Mumeng can have more than a thousand households. On average, each Tusi has more than two thousand households, totaling more than twenty-six thousand households, or more than one hundred and four thousand people.

Religion and Race 100

The local people are very superstitious and like to worship many gods. The Han people mostly believe in Buddhism and Confucianism. The people under the jurisdiction of the Gengma Tusi are even more devout in their beliefs. Children are sent to temples to study Buddhism at the age of six or seven. As for the races, the Han people account for three-tenths of the total population, the Hui people account for two-tenths, and the remaining five-tenths are local indigenous people. Among the indigenous people, there are Baiyi, , Langsu, and tribes. Among them, the Baiyi tribe is mild-mannered and thoughtful, and is gradually merging with the Han people. The , Langsu, and are semi-uncivilized. The Hui people mostly live in the territories under the jurisdiction of the Gangmeng and Gongmeng Tusi. It is said that during the Hong Yang Rebellion, when the Hui people Du Wenxiu's rebellion in Yunnan failed, many Hui people moved from western Yunnan to this area to escape.

Education and Customs 101

Very few of the indigenous people are literate, and they still live a primitive life of recording events by tying knots or carving wood. Only about one or two tenths of the Han and Hui people have received education. The schools are mostly simple, old-style private schools. As for customs, the Han people are influenced by Confucianism, and the Hui people strictly abide by the rules of Muhammad. Therefore, all weddings and funerals are no different from those of the Han and Hui people in the interior, but the forms are slightly simpler. As for the Baiyi, Langsu, and tribes, it is the opposite. Marriage is in the free form of the primitive era. Young men and women often work and sing in the mountains and fields. A kind of popular and loving song is sung, with men singing and women harmonizing, and women singing and men harmonizing. This kind of singing is the medium for the combination of men and women. When they get married, relatives and others gather to celebrate and dance for the newlyweds. However, the Langsu and other tribes have a semi-communal wife system. Funerals include burial, cremation, and wind burial.

Climate and Products 102

The climate varies greatly among the Tusi. The climate in the Menglang and Mengding areas is hot and prone to malaria. Those who contract malaria die within a few hours. The climate in the Gengma and Kokang Tusi is mild, the rains are favorable, and the mountains are clear and the waters are beautiful. Therefore, the population is dense. The products are abundant in all thirteen Tusi. There is plenty of food grain and wheat. There are fierce animals such as bears, deer, tigers, and leopards. There are many silver mines, especially in the Kokang Tusi. The forests are lush, and tea, cotton, and purple stalks are famous. The variety of fruits is also numerous.

Transportation and Commercial Ports 103

Transportation is difficult and travel is not easy. There is a lack of postal and telegraph services. However, the Kokang Tusi has a mild climate and abundant products, and the British forcibly occupied its territory and opened it as a commercial port. The British have established postal and telegraph schools and churches there, and have built automobile roads directly to Burma. When we arrived at the place, we could not help but feel emotional.

The above is a rough overview of the undetermined border section between Yunnan and Burma. Today, the British side is actively invading it, and even regards the area as their own, not allowing our country to interfere. It is hoped that the government and the people will pay special attention to this remote border area.

British Newspaper Discusses China Not Needing to Redeem the Chinese Eastern Railway 104

Just Build a Narrow-Gauge Railway to the Russian Border

Crisis of Russian Invasion Will Be Reduced

Translated by World News Agency: The British newspaper said that the Chinese Eastern Railway once had the opportunity to greatly expand its route, making it the most powerful railway in Manchuria. However, this good opportunity was missed by its director Vorsterloff and the International Technical Committee. They had proposed several plans, such as the Huhu Line, which was later implemented by the Chinese side. The broad gauge used by the Chinese Eastern Railway is gradually becoming useless in Manchuria. In the future, passengers can take through trains directly to the northernmost point of Manchuria from Nanjing or Diankou without changing trains. There are already many signs of this. Recently, the Deputy Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Li Shaogeng, and several Chinese members of the board of directors went to Taonan, ostensibly to celebrate the 90th birthday of Wan Fulin's mother, but in reality, it was related to the railway construction in northern Manchuria. Currently, passengers traveling from southern or central China to the northern Manchurian border must change trains in Shenyang, take the South Manchuria Railway to Changchun, and then take the Chinese Eastern Railway train. However, after the new route to Qiqihar is completed, it is no longer necessary to go to Qiqihar via the South Manchuria Railway or the Chinese Eastern Railway. However, the line must be extended to the Soviet Russian border. The completion of this extension will not only be extremely important for freight transportation but will also have major military implications. By expanding this line to Sakhalin, the Chinese side will be able to reach the Amur River opposite the port of Blagoveshchensk. At the same time, building another line from Hailar westward will allow it to come into contact with the Soviet Russian border at Manzhouli. In this way, in the event of war, Chinese troops can travel from all parts of China directly to the Russian border without changing trains, greatly shortening the time required. At the same time, grain produced in northern Manchuria can be transported directly to the Chinese interior without changing trains. This plan is definitely under discussion now and will be implemented quickly. Once this plan is completed, the value of the Chinese Eastern Railway will be reduced by 50%, because its broad gauge is only useful for through traffic in Russia. Currently, Russia can easily drive its vehicles into Manchuria, but it is impossible to drive them on narrow-gauge. The use of broad gauge on Russian railways was based on the advice of German engineers, who had a deeper meaning. If there were a war, the German side could simply change the Russian gauge to narrow, and German vehicles could enter Russia. Because German vehicles are narrow-gauge and limited by the sleepers, the Russians cannot widen them and drive Russian vehicles into German territory. The same is true for the railway situation between China and Russia in northern Manchuria. The Chinese side only needs to lay a narrow-gauge railway to the border, and the risk of Russian invasion will be reduced. In addition to the western railway construction plan, the Chinese side also plans to build a road from Jilin along the Russian-Mongolian border to the mouth of the Songhua River. The Qiqihar line crosses the Chinese Eastern Railway on the west side, while the Jilin line crosses the Chinese Eastern Railway on the east side. The completion of this line will also greatly affect the transportation of grain to the port of Vladivostok. In short, China does not seem to need to spend millions of dollars to buy the Chinese Eastern Railway. It only needs to spend less than half the purchase price to build new routes on the east and west sides of Manchuria, and the Chinese Eastern Railway will become useless for military purposes against China, and its freight transportation will be reduced by at least half.

Bandits from Puning Retreat to Old Nest in Southern Mountain

Unsuccessful Negotiation between Jiaoji Railway Bureau and Coal Merchants Regarding Freight Rates 106

The Railway Bureau Only Agreed to a Temporary Reduction for Four Months

Coal Merchants Insist on Abolishing the Price Increase Method

Qingdao Correspondence: Zibo, Zhangwei coal merchants, considering the 20% increase in freight rates by the Jiaoji Railway Bureau unbearable, unanimously resolved to suspend operations from May 21st. Previous reports have detailed this. After receiving a telegram from the Coal Industry Joint Association, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau, recognizing the significant impact of a complete shutdown of the coal industry on all aspects, convened a meeting of its members. They telegraphed Boshan, requesting the Joint Association to send representatives to the bureau to negotiate a solution. Upon receiving the telegram, Boshan promptly dispatched eight representatives, who arrived in Qingdao overnight. On the morning of the 19th, at 10 a.m., along with over twenty representatives from the Qingdao coal industry, they attended a meeting at the Jiaoji Railway Bureau. The Railway Bureau expressed partial acceptance of the Joint Association's request and, due to the urgency of the matter, scheduled a follow-up meeting for 6 p.m. that afternoon. At the resumed meeting, the Railway Bureau only agreed to a 20% reduction in inland export prices during the four summer months from June to September. Regarding the cancellation of the price increase, they stated that coal merchants would need to directly petition the government, as the Railway Bureau did not have the authority to decide. The coal merchants argued that the 20% reduction in export coal prices during the four summer months was a long-standing practice and should be implemented as usual, even without the price increase. The method proposed by the Railway Bureau was too far from the original demands of the coal merchants. Furthermore, according to the resolution passed in Boshan, the actions of the coal merchants should be guided by the Joint Association. The representatives immediately telegraphed the Boshan Joint Association to report the progress of the negotiations. At 5 a.m. today, they received a reply from the association, stating that the four-month 20% reduction was a common practice and not a thorough solution. They insisted on suspending operations pending further instructions. At noon, another telegram arrived from Boshan, reiterating the demand to abolish the freight increase. The representatives then returned to the Railway Bureau for further negotiations this afternoon. The Railway Bureau responded that the increase was mandated by the ministry and could not be easily revoked. Since the two sides could not reach an agreement, the representatives left the meeting and returned to Boshan that evening to report everything to the Joint Association. Whether normal transportation will resume remains uncertain. It is also reported that the Shanghai National Coal Production and Sales Joint Association, regarding the issues of increased freight rates on the Jiaoji Railway and the recovery of mining rights, had appointed representatives Yu Shunqing and two others to go to Beijing to petition Commander-in-Chief Chiang and Deputy Commander Zhang. At the same time, they also petitioned the Ministry of Railways to reduce the freight rates for national coal on the Jiaoji Railway, indicating that this issue is not only related to the area along the Jiaoji Railway. Important News 2

Jiangxi Headquarters Approves Anhui Residents to Purchase Rice 107

Lifting the Rice Ban in Leping, Dexing and Other Counties

Wuyuan Correspondence: Wuyuan County, located in the remote border area of southern Anhui, is mountainous and has little arable land. The county's food supply, except for the southwestern townships which are relatively self-sufficient, cannot even provide enough rice for one month's consumption in the northeastern townships. Most of it relies on neighboring counties in Jiangxi, such as Leping, Dexing, Wannian, and Poyang. Since the rampant banditry of the previous year, the water and land transportation between Wuyuan and Jiangxi has been blocked by a small number of troublemakers. After repeated negotiations, it was able to pass. However, the grain-producing areas of Leping and Dexing were then occupied by communist bandits, and transportation was once again cut off. The supply of rice for the people became even more scarce, and the entire county faced a rice shortage for almost a year. Although fellow villagers in Shanghai organized rice relief efforts, the long distance and inconvenience of land transportation made it difficult to provide timely assistance. Fortunately, the southwestern townships had a good rice harvest last year, which averted famine. This year, with the old harvest depleted and the new harvest not yet available, the county public organization, recognizing the food shortage among the military and civilians, raised funds to purchase rice in Wuhu, Jiangxi, and Raozhou. Last month, when the rice was being transported through Xiangtan in Dexing, it was suddenly detained by Xu Jinluo, the county magistrate of Dexing, who firmly refused to release it. Gao, the magistrate of Wuyuan, and various public organizations telegraphed He, the director of the Nanchang headquarters, requesting him to order the county to release the rice and to lift the rice ban in Leping, Dexing, Poyang, and Wannian. They also telegraphed the fellow villagers in Xunyang, requesting them to send representatives to petition the local authorities for relief. The New Anhui fellow villagers in Jiujiang appointed Zhan Mingqiu and Cheng Guangzao as representatives to go to the province to meet with Director He, Chairman Lu, and Minister Wang, to explain the situation. Director He immediately approved the request, telegraphed the Dexing County Magistrate to release the previously detained Wuyuan rice, and authorized the lifting of the rice ban in Leping, Dexing, Poyang, and Wannian, ordering the counties to comply. The memorial of the Xunyang fellow villagers and the instructions of Director He are recorded below: (1) Memorial of the Xunyang Fellow Villagers: "Presenting a memorial regarding the mistaken detention of rice boats, causing starvation among the people of Wuyuan, requesting that the authorities investigate and follow past practices, allowing the limited purchase and transportation of rice to maintain the people's food supply." Wuyuan County is located in a remote border area, surrounded by mountains on three sides. The rugged and steep mountains are as difficult to traverse as the roads of Shu. Only the streams connected to Dexing and Leping in Jiangxi Province are navigable. The main products are vegetables. The county's own grain production can only supply food for three months. The rest relies on counties such as Dexing, Leping, Wannian, and Poyang to survive, requiring approximately 5,000 shi of rice per month. This has been the case for centuries. In the past, when Jiangxi banned rice exports, Wuyuan was treated the same and allowed to continue transporting rice as usual. This is the special situation of Wuyuan's insufficient grain supply, which relies on Dexing and Leping. The waterways of Dexing and Leping are the lifeline of Wuyuan, and this is the only route for transportation in and out. In recent years, banditry has been frequent, and there have been successive droughts and floods, causing hundreds of thousands of people to suffer. Now, the area is a bandit suppression zone, and the troops stationed in Wuyuan are lacking food, causing even greater panic. If the source of food is cut off, hundreds of thousands of people will either die at the hands of bandits or starve to death. The Wuyuan Chamber of Commerce, recognizing this, has raised funds to purchase rice and grains in Dexing, Leping, Wannian, Poyang and other counties, selling them at a fair price, purely to maintain the daily food supply of the military and civilians and is not involved in commercial activities. The county is located inland, and the mountain roads are rugged, making it impossible to transport the rice to other places. This is not comparable to coastal ports on the Yangtze River, which have no restrictions. The Dexing County Magistrate, without investigating the special situation of Wuyuan's food supply and misunderstanding the strict order from the government prohibiting large-scale commercial rice exports, did not first present the special situation for instructions but immediately stopped the rice, disregarding the hundreds of thousands of people in Wuyuan. Even in times of famine, international law does not allow the embargo of grain. Moreover, these are neighboring counties belonging to the same national government, and there should be no distinction between regions. In addition to appointing Zhan Mingqiu and Cheng Guangzao as representatives to petition the authorities to explain everything, we hereby submit this memorial, requesting your government to consider the imminent starvation of hundreds of thousands of people in Wuyuan, quickly order the Dexing County government to release the rice that was previously detained, and allow the limited monthly purchase of rice to relieve the people's food supply. We are waiting anxiously for your orders." (2) Response from the Headquarters: "Received and noted. Regarding the food shortage in Wuyuan, the county magistrate and various public organizations have previously telegraphed reports. The headquarters has already considered the situation to be factual and has authorized the lifting of the rice ban in Leping and Dexing, Jiangxi, and ordered the release of the previously detained rice boats to provide relief. A separate telegram has been sent for compliance. You are hereby notified." (May 13)

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs Protects the Cocoon Market 108

Jiangsu Province has always produced a large quantity of silkworm cocoons, which are of great importance to the national economy and the people's livelihood. Therefore, the provincial government has always had special plans to protect the cocoon season. Now that bandits are rampant and robberies are frequent, it is even more important to be careful in providing protection. The Provincial Department of Civil Affairs has revised seven articles of the protection measures and seven articles of the regional patrol plan, ordering subordinates to comply and sending letters to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters and the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office for review. A request has also been submitted to the provincial government to forward it to the Pacification Superintendent to order subordinates to review. The protection measures for the cocoon market and the regional patrol plan are recorded below.

Measures for Protecting the Cocoon Market 109

(Article 1) The protection of the cocoon market shall be jointly undertaken by the Provincial Water Police Force and the stationed army. However, for the sake of careful protection, an office should be established in Wuxi County, where the cocoon market is most prosperous, as per previous practice. The district chief of the second district of the Provincial Water Police Force shall go there to command. (Article 2) The office shall be supplied with twenty patrol boats from each of the first and third districts of the Provincial Water Police Force, and a number of patrol ships shall be dispatched by the department to respond to requests for protection from cocoon merchants and to be dispatched at any time. (Article 3) The location and number of cocoon shops, as well as the opening date, shall be notified to the office by the Cocoon Industry Association in advance to facilitate unified protection. (Article 4) In the areas where cocoon shops are located, the land shall be guarded by troops stationed, and the water shall be patrolled by ships dispatched by the Provincial Water Police Force. (Article 5) When cocoon shops transport funds by land, the army shall send troops to escort them. When transporting funds by water, the office or the nearby Provincial Water Police Force shall send ships to escort them. If it is necessary to transport funds by both land and water, the army and the Provincial Water Police Force shall alternate in escorting them. However, the cocoon merchants shall notify the amount of funds, the starting and ending points, the places of exchange, and the dates in advance to ensure thoroughness. (Article 6) At major ports and in areas where the cocoon market is prosperous, the stationed army and the office shall dispatch troops and ships to patrol back and forth day and night to show seriousness. (Article 7) All military police officers and soldiers responsible for protection shall not solicit rewards from the cocoon merchants. If there is any violation, the cocoon merchants are allowed to report to the office at any time and be punished separately after reporting.

Regional Patrol Plan 110

(Article 1) The counties of Songjiang, Shanghai, Fengxian, Jinshan, and Jiading shall be responsible for the first district of the Provincial Water Police Force in cooperation with the stationed army. (Article 2) The counties of Wuxi, Wujin, Yixing, and part of Jiangyin County, as well as the eastern and western mountains of Taihu Lake, shall be responsible for the second district of the Provincial Water Police Force in cooperation with the stationed army and patrol ships. (Article 3) The counties of Changshu, Kunshan, Wujiang, Wuxian, etc., and the border between Jiangsu and Zhejiang shall be responsible for the third district of the Provincial Water Police Force in cooperation with the stationed army. (Article 4) The area of Baoshan County shall be responsible for the fourth district of the Provincial Water Police Force in cooperation with the stationed army. (Article 5) Part of Jiangyin County and the counties of Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jiangning, and Yangzhou shall be responsible for the fifth district of the Provincial Water Police Force in cooperation with the stationed army. (Article 6) The Provincial Water Police Force, guerrillas, and patrol ships shall be dispatched to patrol along different routes to supplement the insufficient police force. (Article 7) The department designates the district chief of the second district of the Provincial Water Police Force to organize an office in Wuxi, where the cocoon market is prosperous, to supervise and command. (May 22)

The Trial Process of the Xu Zhuoran Assassination Case by the Hangzhou Court 111

The assassination case of Xu Zhuoran in Xiamen, involving the former principal of Jimei School, Ye Caizhen, has been transferred to the Hangzhou Court for trial by the judicial authorities. It is reported that the Hangzhou Court has summoned various witnesses and held multiple hearings. There is no evidence regarding the accusation against Ye for murder. Chen Delin, who confessed to Ye's murder in the Tong'an Corps, has confessed in both the Xiamen and Hangzhou courts that the confession was obtained through torture by the Corps. The evidence presented by Ye's side also showed that he was not at the school on the day Chen claimed he negotiated at the school and the day the suspects handed over the money. Moreover, of the three suspects confessed by Chen, Lin Min was beaten to death in September of the seventeenth year. The Hangzhou Court entrusted the Siming Court to verify the fact, and it was confirmed that Lin Min was dead and could not have committed the murder in the nineteenth year. Based on the above circumstances, the case could have been concluded earlier. However, it is said that one or two military authorities have repeatedly sent telegrams to the Hangzhou Court to argue, which has delayed the resolution of the case.

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 112

Remnants of Taibao A Shu Rise Again to Form Gangs 113

Since the execution of Taibao A Shu, the ringleader of the Taihu bandits, Xu A Da, the remaining bandit leader, has recently led over two hundred men to areas around the Three Hills Gate, Lake Mouth, and Yangcheng Lake in Taihu Lake, attempting to revive the gang. Yesterday, Commander Zhu of the Suzhou-Changzhou Pacification Command telegraphed the county government, ordering the police force to cooperate with the water police and Gao's battalion, stationed in Zhenze Town, Wujiang, to jointly suppress the bandits and eliminate the threat.

Details of the Robbery in the Suzhou Countryside 114

The following are the details of the case of lake bandits continuously robbing and killing in the Shiqiao Town, Lu Mu area of the Suzhou countryside. Wang Chuantou (Wang Boatman) is about 30 li from the Lu Mu area office, with 30-50 merchants, mostly wealthy. There are brothers surnamed Shen, the elder brother Zhu Rong, who practices medicine in Shanghai, and the younger brother Zhu Ling, who practices medicine at home. They are extremely wealthy in land property, and the area is quite prominent. The area is about 4-5 li from Lu She in Changshu, separated by only one river. On the other side is Xinzhuang. Previously, on the 20th, the Yue Temple festival in Changshu was very popular, and the bandit scouts took the opportunity to gamble, observing the wealth of the residents based on the size of the gambling wins and losses, in preparation for the robbery. In the evening, after the residents of Wang Chuantou returned from the festival, several bandit ships carrying over a hundred bandits armed with weapons sailed from Yangcheng Lake to Yaojia浜 in Shiqiao Town, Huangdai area. They landed from the east and invaded the home of Xu Nancun, the village head of Gate No. 2, tying up Xu and his wife and two sons. Then, they went to the home of Xu Ruichen, kidnapping his son Rong Sheng. At the same time, another group of over fifty people went to No. 2, Lu Jia Li, nearby, kidnapping four residents: Lu Gunguan, Lu Abao, Lu Amao, and Lu Shunsheng. When the neighbor Lu Shansheng sounded the alarm on the roof, he was shot and killed by the bandits, who dragged the body away and also shot Lu Genbao. At 3 a.m. on the 21st, the bandits again raided Wang Chuantou in Lu Mu. At that time, Shen Zhuling's mother had gone to relatives in Changshu city, and Shen's wife had taken her two sons to Xinzhuang. Only Shen himself was at home taking care of the house because he needed to see patients. A group of about twenty bandits, all armed with pistols, iron rulers, and flashlights, directly surrounded Shen's house. Shen was awakened from his sleep, and he quickly climbed onto the roof and knocked on an oil drum to sound the alarm. The bandits used a large stone to break down the gate, tied up Shen, and forced him to reveal where the money was hidden. As a result, all the valuables in the house were robbed. All those with any wealth in the village were also robbed. Before leaving, they took Shen to a bandit ship, entered Yangcheng Lake, and left. At the same time, Liu Jinrong, a merchant from Shanghai, had returned home to see the festival. Because he was wearing nice clothes, he was also kidnapped.

Telegram Requesting Strict Punishment of Robbers on the Shanghai-Nanjing Train 115

The Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce, based on reports that three robbers on the Shanghai-Nanjing train near Kunshan pushed a young female passenger off the train, causing her to fall to her death, intending to rob her of her belongings, were stopped by another passenger who frantically blew the whistle, resulting in the arrest of the three robbers by the railway police, stated that such incidents of robbery and murder in the crowded Shanghai-Nanjing train should not be tolerated. If they are not severely punished, it would not be enough to deter the bandits. Therefore, on the 22nd, they telegraphed the Capital Garrison Headquarters, requesting them to order the Railway Guard Corps to severely punish the bandits to deter them.

Wuxi

Bandits Rob 13 Families Consecutively 116

Thirteen families in Xizhang Tao Lane, the 16th district of the county, including Tao Buyun, Tao Shunfa, Tao Genrong, Tao Jinpan, Tao Aquan, Tao Agou, Tao Jinfa, Tao Xingquan, Zhu Jinchuan, etc., are all farmers and in very poor circumstances. After 1 a.m. the night before, suddenly over twenty bandits armed with weapons arrived, first going to Tao Buyun's house, breaking down the door and entering, tying up Buyun and his wife, and beating them severely with iron rods, causing serious injuries and endangering their lives. The bandits searched for a long time, but finding nothing of value, went one by one to the homes of Tao Shunfa and others, searching each house. After four hours, they still found nothing, so they shouted slogans such as "Big bad luck" and set off firecrackers, escaping in a southeastern direction. Afterwards, Yuan Zishun, the leader of the first squad of the sixth team of the second district of the water police stationed there, led armed police officers to investigate and pursue, but the bandits had already fled far away. Tao Buyun and his wife, who were injured, were unable to pay for medical treatment. Yuan gave them five yuan for medical expenses and sent them to the city hospital for treatment.

Summary of Resolutions of the County Party Consolidation Meeting 117

The County Party Consolidation Meeting held its 113th committee meeting yesterday, chaired by Hu Nianqian. The following is a summary of the important resolutions: 1. The Third District Party Department presented a case requesting the transfer to the court for the detention of Chen Fengyi, a local rogue who falsely accused Jiang Bosen, and requesting severe punishment according to law. Resolved: Order Jiang Bosen to file a lawsuit with the court according to law, and then review the matter. 2. The Second Direct District Branch presented a case regarding Wang Jinwen, also known as Wang Genbao, a member of the Axe Gang, who has committed numerous crimes and engaged in illicit activities, requesting a letter be sent to the County Anti-Banditry Bureau for strict investigation. Resolved: Wang Jinwen has been sent to the County Court, and the County Anti-Banditry Bureau should be asked to transfer him for interrogation. 3. City citizens Xue Junhou and others presented a case regarding the Jisheng Han boats, which were carrying passengers beyond their capacity, requesting the county government to promptly stop their operation to avoid danger. Resolved: The case will be approved and notified. 4. Hu Yunji and others from the paper-making industry presented a case regarding Zhang Zheng and others from the paper-making industry, who were falsely organizing an industry association, requesting an investigation and correction. Resolved: Handed over to the training official for investigation and handling. 5. Assistant staff member Ma Tingdong reported back on the investigation of Hu Yiqing and others' accusation against Hua Juquan regarding the construction of a dangerous earth field, requesting review. Resolved: Send a letter to the Construction Bureau for separate handling. 6. Zhang Naijun and others from the Investment Bureau presented a case regarding Mu Mingshu's non-compliance with regulations in construction, encroaching on public land and obstructing water and land transportation, requesting a transfer for rectification. Resolved: Send a letter to the Construction Bureau for thorough investigation and response. 7. The County Construction Bureau sent a letter explaining the circumstances of Qian Zhaoyi's building permit transfer, requesting review. Resolved: The reply is inconsistent with the facts, and a letter should be sent to the bureau again, requesting a revised demolition plan and its thorough implementation.

Results of the Party Ideology Advancement Competition 118

The county's Party Ideology Speech Competition was held at the Zhongnan Grand Theater at 9 a.m. the day before. There were representatives from over fifty groups and over a thousand guests. Hu Nianqian, the standing committee member of the County Party Committee, presided over the meeting, performing the customary rituals. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the preparatory process. Then, Yi Zuolin, the provincial inspector judge, delivered a speech. Then, seven speakers, including Ms. Yang Yueshou, Zong Yongsun, Zeng Lu Jiang Zhida, Ms. Zou Xiangsun, Zhu Yuchang, and Ms. Yi Shunying, selected from the announced topics, one by one, gave their speeches in the competition. The speakers' great arguments and eloquence were extremely incisive and moving. After the competition, three judges, including Provincial Inspector Yi Zuolin, Wang Maozu of Suzhou Middle School, and Chen Yunyi, the principal of Suzhou Girls' Middle School, made their evaluations. As a result, Ms. Yang Yueshou of Jingzhi Girls' School won first place, Song Yongsun won second place, and Zeng Lu won third place. Others, such as Zhu Yuchang, Xiao Xiangsun, and Jiang Zhida, also scored well. Later, County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia, representing Gu Cheng, went on stage to give awards separately to encourage them.

The county had previously requested the financial department to approve the additional collection of five li in the deed tax item because the household registration expenses could not be obtained through other means. The department has now issued an order stating, "Considering that the number of people who have the ability to purchase property is still small, approval is granted to proceed accordingly. Please comply accordingly." After receiving the order from the county government, it was decided to collect the fees starting from June 1st.

Regarding the case of the Japanese ship Yijin Maru colliding with and sinking the Xu Huiyuan cargo ship on the Ren Gang River, the county government reported it to the provincial government. According to instructions, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has been consulted to negotiate with the Japanese consulate.

Peace and Tranquility Along the Coastal Waters of Northern Jiangsu 121

The coastal waters of northern Jiangsu Province were not peaceful. After the joint efforts of the naval and land forces, police, and the bandit suppression team, as of the 21st, the banditry has been completely suppressed, according to the radio report from the bandit suppression police ship. The remaining bandits fled to the Shandong waters on seven ships. The Fishery Protection Office established in Tongcheng is currently rushing to complete its closure. The Jiangsu Maritime Guerrilla Force under Shen Fengshan, which was incorporated by the Provincial Security Office, will soon be inspected at the Haikou area of Taizhou.

Pinghu

Suspect Bandit Sent Back to the County for Investigation 122

Fu A Huan, the cousin of the infamous bandit Fu Jichang from Pinghu, was suspected of colluding with bandits. He was previously arrested by the Inland River Police Bureau and sent to Hangzhou for legal action. Now, it is learned that the village committee has submitted a letter to Hangzhou proving that Fu A Huan is indeed a law-abiding citizen and requesting his release. The request has been approved by the Water Police Bureau, and he was sent back to the county yesterday for verification and handling.

Abductor Arrested at Xitang Bridge 123

Ni Siguan, a farmer in Yinxing Village, married Jiang, and their relationship was known to be harmonious. However, Ni Xiaoer, an abductor, coveted Jiang's good looks and tried to abduct her. He successfully seduced her, and they agreed to run away. After abducting her, the abductor colluded with his uncle, Mr. Jia, to sell her, splitting the profits. The day before yesterday, Ni Siguan received a report that the abductors were negotiating a price at Xitang Bridge and were about to complete the transaction. Siguan rushed there and found his wife Jiang and Ni Xiaoer, etc., all in one place. He immediately alerted the police, who arrested them and took them into custody for questioning.

Jiaxing

Bandits Involved in the Jin Liujiu Kidnapping Case Arrested 124

The Xincheng Fourth Section Anti-Banditry Office in Jiaxing learned that the kidnapping and ransom case of Jin Liujiu, a Shaoxing merchant residing in the Dongzha area of Xincheng, was actually related to Qian Ahu from Qianjia Bridge and Chen Youcai from Lailong Bridge, both located nearby. The day before yesterday, they managed to arrest these two men. After repeated interrogation, they confessed that the bandit leader was Pan (from Pudong, Shanghai), who lived in Hongyang Port and had 700-800 followers. In addition to selling smuggled salt, they were also kidnappers. The section office also cooperated with the military police to search their residences, but the bandits had already escaped after hearing the news. The two criminals, Qian Ahu and Chen Youcai, were sent to the County Anti-Banditry Office for interrogation and handling.

Hangzhou

Car Accident on the Hangzhou-Yuyao Highway 125

Yesterday at 11 a.m., a bus of the Hangzhou-Yuyao Highway Bus Company, when driving near the Madeng Bridge in Songmuchang, crashed into a rice field due to the driver's carelessness, and the bus overturned and fell into the mud. Eight passengers were injured, one of whom had a serious hand injury. The driver telegraphed the station manager, who dispatched another bus to the scene to transport the injured to the hospital for treatment.

###浦江 Bandit Leader Escorted to the Province

The bandit leader Zhen Guorong from the eastern township of Pujiang County, last October, led a gang of bandits to loot the home of Zhen Jiyao, the village head of Zhen Village, completely. He then secretly traveled to Hangzhou, changed his name to Zhen Ziming, and joined a certain army unit as a soldier. Before half a month had passed, he conspired with his fellow villager Hong Yiguo and absconded with two wooden-cased pistols. He returned to his hometown and shot and killed Zhen Jiyao, but had not been apprehended. Unexpectedly, on the 19th of this month, the bandit was found hiding in Changhua.

He communicated with Zhang Yingye, the leader of the "Invincible Bandit Gang" of the same county, who was detained in the army prison. The letter was intercepted, and the Security Office immediately dispatched personnel to secretly arrest him. Before that, the bandit had changed his name to Zhu Zhirong and resided in a hotel. Due to his suspicious behavior, he was detained by the Changhua County Public Security Bureau. On the 20th, he was escorted to the provincial capital and transferred to the Provincial Bandit Suppression Bureau. On the 21st, he was sent to the army prison for strict handling.

Accidental Ingestion of Pills Leads to Fatal Poisoning 126

Wang Yongquan, a tanner by trade, near Yue Tomb in West Lake, recently suffered from leucorrhea. He purchased a dose of pills from Wang Youcai near the Diaojiao Bridge at Wulin Gate. After taking them home and swallowing them, his face became swollen and blue. Soon after, all his teeth fell out, and he could not speak. He died of poisoning yesterday. After neighbors reported to the Sixth Precinct of the Second District, a sanitary police officer was dispatched to investigate. A few small remaining pills were taken back and submitted to the Public Security Bureau for chemical testing to investigate the matter.

Ningbo

Robbers Burn and Loot, Killing People 127

In the Xu Mazhan area of Lianshan, Fenghua County, at 12:00 PM the night before last, suddenly sixty to seventy robbers arrived. They first set fire to the village as a show of force, then went to Wang Xingjun's house and kidnapped his six-year-old son. The village defense team heard the alarm and went to rescue him, but they were outnumbered and had several firearms seized by the bandits. A villager, named Jia, assisted in capturing the bandits but was shot and killed by them. Also, in Huangshakeng in the western township of Fenghua, a remote area with few residents,

around midnight the night before last, fifty to sixty robbers also arrived. They first burned down all the houses in the village, then took the opportunity to loot everything they could and left. The village head, Wang Guozhen, entered the city yesterday and reported to the county government to dispatch troops to pursue them.

Kaiming Bridge Church Burned Down 128

The Sheng Kung Hui (Anglican) Church on Kaiming Bridge in Yubu City, which housed the Feidi Primary School, was home to principal Jin Tirong and his family in the side room on the left of the church for twenty years. Unexpectedly, at 2:30 AM this morning (the 21st), a fire suddenly broke out in the firewood shed. The fire was very intense, and it was only extinguished after the fire brigades fought bravely to put it out. Six buildings were burned down, resulting in significant losses. Fortunately, the buildings were surrounded by walls, preventing the fire from spreading to neighboring residences.

Xiaoshan

Cocoon Tax Changed to Business Tax 129

Yesterday, the Xiaoshan County Government received a provincial telegram stating that the cocoon tax should be changed to a business tax. A public notice was issued to the cocoon merchants in various towns and villages, stating that according to the provincial telegram, the cocoon tax, which Zhejiang Province has always collected, should no longer be collected this year in accordance with the central government's order to abolish transit taxes. The business tax to be collected will be based on the tax rate set by the ministry, which is only 2/1000, a very light burden. As for the local funds contributed by cocoon merchants in various cities and counties, since they are not in the nature of transit taxes and are related to local donations, they should still be donated by the cocoon merchants as usual to maintain them.

Husband and Wife Quarrel, Commit Suicide in Succession 130

Zhou Weishun, a fisherman living outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan, on Dongdai, quarreled with his wife, Guo, because his son did not engage in proper work. His wife, Guo, was naturally hot-tempered. On the 20th of this month, the couple quarreled again. At night, his wife clapped her hands on the table and cursed loudly. Weishun, feeling that his reputation was at stake, did not dare to go home. That night, it happened to be raining, so he threw himself into the river and drowned. The next morning, his body floated to the surface. His wife met him at the riverbank and deeply regretted her actions. On the night of the 23rd, she also hanged herself. Neighbors discovered this and tried to rescue her, but it was too late.

Zhou Taixing and Xiao Dong Abducted in Dayi 131

Zhou Abing's six-year-old son, the owner of the Dayi and Taixing grocery store in the eastern township of Xiaoshan, was kidnapped by five bandits on the night of the 15th. On the night of the 18th, a letter was received from Shanghai demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan, to be paid within half a month. The family is now extremely anxious because they cannot raise the funds.

Bengbu

The Opium Scourge in Various Counties of Northern Anhui 132

The opium scourge in northern Anhui has been poisoning the region for many years. The authorities have long adopted a policy of disguising prohibition as taxation, which has only served to exacerbate the problem. Wei Lihuang, the commander of the Northern Anhui Garrison, in order to eradicate the opium scourge, strictly ordered the counties to prohibit it in September and promulgated four articles of punitive regulations, with violators subject to military law. However, in counties such as Su, Si, Meng, Wo, Hao, Fu, Ying, and Tai, greedy and foolish people still secretly planted opium. In recent months, the poisonous flowers have flourished, filling the fields. Some officials and gentry in several counties have even implemented registration and collected seedling taxes, with some counties charging opium seedling taxes of more than ten to seventy yuan per mu. A few days ago, a certain county magistrate, so-and-so, summoned the district chiefs and ordered them to acknowledge an opium tax of 300,000 yuan, or face imprisonment. Such stories are shocking, but they are common in northern Anhui and are not surprising. Wei Lihuang has recently received repeated reports of counties registering and collecting seedling taxes without authorization. A few days ago, he sent telegrams to the county magistrates of Fuyang, Hao County, Woyang, Taihe, Yingshang, Su County, and Si County, ordering them to thoroughly investigate and report within five days to facilitate verification and handling. He also sent telegrams to the county party departments in the aforementioned counties, instructing them to report any information they may have obtained as soon as possible.

Letter

Letter from Zhang Pengchao 133

Dear Editor, I was shocked to read the news item entitled "Red Bandit Zhang Pengchao and Others Apprehended" in the local correspondence column of your newspaper on May 15th. The content of the report is completely inconsistent with the facts. Zhang Pengchao and others have served the local community for many years. They were previously framed and falsely accused by local petty criminals and recently came to the provincial capital to defend themselves and await trial. Furthermore, the County Chamber of Commerce, Farmers' Association, Financial Management Office, District Office, standing brigades, and various organizations of the county have dispatched representatives Qin Tichen and Yang Juchen to the provincial capital to present the circumstances of Zhang Pengchao and others being wrongly accused to the Anhui Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, and the Military Law Review Board. I believe that the truth of this case will be easily resolved. I am deeply concerned that the rumors are untrue and will confuse public opinion. I am writing to request that your newspaper correct the record. Zhang Pengchao, Wu Jingxiu, Hua Kaihao, and others from Yuyi County, May 21st.

Education News

Important News 134

Fifth Pacific Science Congress 135

China Sends Personnel to Prepare to Participate

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has recently approved a communication from the British Minister to China, Lampson, stating that the Fifth Pacific Science Congress, at the request of the Canadian government, is scheduled to be held in Victoria and Vancouver in June 1932. The Congress is composed of representatives from scientific societies affiliated with the Pacific Science Association, which was established in 1920. Its purpose is to promote cooperation on scientific issues in the Pacific region, particularly those related to the prosperity and well-being of the people of the Pacific. The National Research Council of Canada, which is affiliated with the Science Association, is preparing all aspects of the Congress. The Minister hereby represents the Research Council in inviting the Chinese government to send representatives to participate. Furthermore, since the China Science Society in Nanjing has previously represented China at the Honolulu Science Association, the invitation should be conveyed to the staff of the Society. The Congress is prepared to host ten official representatives from the Chinese government and the China Science Society. Additional unofficial representatives and representatives from other organizations are welcome to participate, but they must bear their own expenses. After approving the communication, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs requested the Ministry of Education to consider and respond. The Ministry of Education, noting that the previous Pacific Science Congress was attended by representatives from the Academia Sinica, considered this matter to be the same and sent a letter to the Academia Sinica requesting it to prepare to select representatives to attend. It is reported that the Academia Sinica had already made plans for the Congress and had appointed members of the various committees of the Preparatory Committee to prepare and plan immediately in order to ensure perfection. The list of members of the Preparatory Committee for the Fifth Pacific Science Congress is recorded below: Chen Zongyi (Agriculture), Song Chunfang (Oceanography), Zhang Xinyi (Agriculture), Weng Wenhao (Standing Committee Member and Geology), Bingzhi (Standing Committee Member and Zoology), Li Siguang (Physics), Qian Chongshu (Botany), Li Ji (Anthropology), Hu Xian (Botany), Jiang Bingran (Meteorology and Oceanography), Zhu Kezhen (Standing Committee Member and Meteorology), Ministry of Education.

Explanation of the Powers of the Executive Secretary of the Educational Association 136

The Ministry of Education, based on a report from the Anhui Provincial Department of Education regarding a request from the Chuxian County Educational Association for an explanation of the powers of the executive secretary, instructed the Department as follows: The report has been noted. The powers of the executive secretary of the County Educational Association should be comparable to those of the executive director of the Provincial Educational Association under Article 22 of the Educational Association Law, and his powers are to perform routine affairs. You are hereby informed to acknowledge this and to instruct accordingly.

Local News

Starting June 10th 137

Review of Qualifications of Party Teachers 138

Party-Educational Institutions Organize Qualification Review Committee for Party Teachers

Party ideology teachers and deans of students at all levels of schools in this city have been appointed only after being certified by the Party Ideology Teacher Certification Committee jointly established by the Training Department of the Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Bureau of Education. Since its implementation, the committee has certified four sessions, totaling about two hundred people, which has yielded significant results. However, the Central Government previously found that the certification system had shortcomings, so it formulated an overall plan, which was approved by the Central Standing Committee. It issued the Provisional Regulations for Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers and the Organizational Regulations for the Qualification Review Committee for Party Ideology Teachers, ordering party committees at all levels to organize committees with the local educational administrative agencies to handle the review matters in their respective areas in accordance with the law. All previous certification regulations were abolished. After receiving the order, the Municipal Executive Committee and the Training Department began preparations. The Training Department drafted the Provisional Regulations for Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers in Shanghai Municipality, the Organizational Regulations for the Qualification Review Committee for Party Ideology Teachers in Shanghai Municipality, and the list of committee members. These were approved by the 100th session of the Executive Committee and then submitted to the Central Training Department for approval. Letters of appointment were issued to formally appoint the committee members. The list of committee members is as follows: Jiang Huaishu (alternate supervisory member of the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee), Zhu Jiarang (chief executive of the Party Ideology Education Section of the Municipal Training Department), Wu Xianren (chief executive of the Party Member Training Section of the Municipal Training Department), Wang Manyun (chief executive of the General Affairs Section of the Municipal Training Department), Yuan Yeyu (editor of the Republic Daily), Yang Peiwen (staff member of the Municipal Bureau of Education), Chen Duanzhi (staff member of the Municipal Bureau of Education). After the Qualification Review Committee for Party Ideology Teachers in this city was organized in accordance with the law, all work was handled by the Party Ideology Education Section of the Municipal Training Department. However, since the committee's organization was originally based on a committee system, it was necessary to elect standing committee members to oversee the work and to ensure that the important regulations and methods were decided by the committee in accordance with the law. Therefore, the first meeting was held at the Municipal Party Committee at 1:00 PM yesterday. The committee members present were Yang Peiwen, Chen Duanzhi, Wu Xianren, Wang Manyun, Zhu Jiarang, and Jiang Huaishu. Zhu Jiarang was elected as the chairman. The important resolutions are recorded below: 1. Zhu Jiarang was elected as the standing committee member. 2. The Shanghai Municipality Regulations for Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Ideology Teachers were approved. 3. The Detailed Rules for the Operation of the Qualification Review Committee for Party Ideology Teachers in Shanghai Municipality were approved. 4. The Meeting Rules for the Qualification Review Committee for Party Ideology Teachers in Shanghai Municipality were approved. 5. The Shanghai Municipality Party Ideology Teacher Qualification Review Form (including the application form and curriculum vitae) was approved. The starting and ending dates for the first review of Party ideology teachers were determined to be from June 10th to September 10th, a period of three months. 7. A request will be submitted to the Municipal Executive Committee for the issuance of an official seal. It is reported that all Party ideology teachers or deans of students in all schools in the city, regardless of whether they have been previously certified, must apply to the committee for review or registration in accordance with the law and obtain a certificate.

The Aftermath for Students of Nanyang Medical College

National and Provincial Colleges Should Accept All Qualified Students 139

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has reported to the Ministry of Education the case of the Shanghai Private Nanyang Medical College Student Screening Committee's report on the students' screening results and the related aftermath issues. The Ministry of Education's directive No. 1642 states: All documents have been noted. Regarding the aftermath of this case, the plan proposed by the committee in item B should be approved. (That is, students who have passed the screening and are determined to be promising, and who are willing to extend their study period and have passed the entrance examination, may be given the opportunity to transfer to national medical colleges. (However, those with scores above 50 may transfer at their original grade level, those with scores from 35 to 50 will be demoted one year, and those with scores below 35 will be demoted two years.) In addition to the Ministry issuing an order to national, provincial, and registered private universities and colleges with medical colleges or departments to accept all qualified students during enrollment, you are hereby ordered to inform the relevant students of the former Nanyang College to comply.

Liangjiang Girls' School

Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team's Eastern Expedition Diary (7) 147

(Sent by Huang Jiping from Korea on the 17th)

27-16 Victory Over Tongde Girls' High School 148

(Seoul Correspondence) After arriving in Seoul, Korea, on the 14th, the Liangjiang Girls' School basketball team rested for one day due to the fatigue of traveling. On the afternoon of the 16th, they held their first match against the Tongde Girls' High School basketball team. The location was the Seoul Sports Ground. Chinese and Japanese national flags were hung at the entrance, fluttering in the wind. The flags of the Korean News Agency, which hosted the event, were hung around the perimeter of the field. The event was heavily decorated as a promotional opportunity for the agency. There were more than 2,000 spectators, with Chinese expatriates and students on the right, Japanese expatriates on the left, and Korean students and civilians on both sides, all cheering enthusiastically. The crowd regarded this as an unprecedented grand event in the Korean Peninsula's sports scene. The team entered the field at 4:30 PM. The players of both teams stood side by side, and Kwon, the president of the Korean News Agency, delivered the opening speech, explaining the significance of initiating an international women's sports competition and expressing the hope that they would jointly promote the spirit of sportsmanship. Vice President Mushe of the Korean Sports Association and Ji Damin, the Acting Consul General of our country, delivered speeches successively, expressing their sincerity. The match began at 5:10 PM. Watanabe and Kasaya served as referees. The match ended at 6:00 PM. Liangjiang won a major victory over Tongde with a score of 27-16. The scores for each quarter are as follows: First Quarter 10-5, Second Quarter 13-1, Third Quarter 3-1, Fourth Quarter 1-9.

Looking at the situation of both sides in the war, the Liangjiang team worked hard in the first half of the match, unanimously using contact skills. The ball was contested and stolen, causing the other party to be timid. The Tongde team's movements were slow, their passing was lacking, and they always felt stretched, making it difficult to develop. In the last five minutes of the second half, the Korean audience cheered loudly and enthusiastically supported the Tongde players, who took a deep breath and fought desperately. Taking advantage of the Liangjiang team's fatigue, they even scored a few goals. However, the result was still more than ten points apart. Tongde was not an enemy of Liangjiang. In this battle, Liangjiang's Shao Jinying greatly showed her skills, scoring fourteen points alone. Indeed, so-called three-point division has its ground. Li Yiyun is really heroic!

Suzhou Women's Sports Meet Held This Morning 149

In the past, Suzhou's sports achievements had no record at all. "Because they are Suzhou Misses" has also become synonymous with weakness. After Xu Minhui, the coach of Soochow University, and Ms. Lin Yunsheng, the coach of Suzhou Women's Middle School, initiated the organization of the Women's Sports Association in 1929, they initially engaged in the promotion of ball games. In 1930, they held an athletics competition once. Thanks to the efforts of the sports community, both provincial sports meets came back with banners. Therefore, the name of Suzhou Miss was changed to become the focus of the sports community of the whole province. Now, this year's women's track and field competition will be held at the Zhu Jiazhuang Cheng Lie Special Stadium at 9:00 AM today. Preparations have already been completed. Tickets have been sold in advance and have been very popular. On the day of the event, the results will be broadcasted by the Suzhou Da Su Tong News Agency through the Guo Hua Electric Radio Station. It is certain that Cheng Lie, Zhuang Mingzhen, Zhang Maolan and Zhu Guoying of Suzhou Women's Middle School will have excellent results. However, it is a pity that Miss Zhang of the Women's Middle School was injured in the leg during the last provincial sports meet and has not yet recovered. Those with good skills do not know whether they can be addicted to sports enthusiasts.

Finals Report

16-Pound Shot Put 157

Leng Peigen of Jinling won first place in the third attempt of the final with 9.92 meters. The results were average. In the competition of nine people, the highest score in the preliminary round was Leng Peigen's 9.62 meters. In the final, Chen Guoxiang of Soochow progressed to 9.64 meters to get second place. Hu Minteng of Hujiang's 9.425 meters ranked third as a preliminary round result. Liu Xingqian of Hujiang ranked fourth with a score of 9.35 meters. The ground was slippery after the rain, so the results were not particularly outstanding.

Long Jump 158

During the long jump final, there were surprises and joys. Ling Yuanchang of Jinling, the defending champion, did not exceed six meters in five jumps, while Wang Pusheng of University of Shanghai took the lead with 5.97 meters. Unexpectedly, in the last attempt of Ling Yuanyang alone, he jumped out six meters and suddenly took first place. The result was 6.19 meters. The results were average. The second place and below were all less than six meters. It may be because the run-up was loose. There were few other changes during the game.

1500 Meters 159

Nine people started. At 400 meters, Xia Xianzhuan of Shanghai led, with Meng Guangxin of Jinling closely following. Then Zhan Zongyi and Yu Xin accelerated. Meng Guangxin of Jinling sped up, and at 800 meters, he was already ahead of Xia Xianzhuan. At this time, Huang Dexing of Soochow was also gradually catching up. At 1200 meters, Meng Guangxin increased his speed, Xia Xianzhuan fell behind by 30 meters, and Huang Dexing of Soochow caught up to fourth place. In the final 300 meters, Meng Guangxin sprinted and took first place with a time of four minutes and forty-eight and five-tenths seconds. Xia Xianzhuan was still 50 meters behind. Huang Dexing crossed the line almost simultaneously with Xia, separated by a shoulder. Zhan Zongyi took fourth place.
